class="Card-content"><p>Configurar git</p>

<p>Git add .</p>

<p>Git status</p>

<p>Esto borrar todos los branches, commits, stashes etc.</p></div></div><div class="Card-bottom"><div class="Card-bottom-left"><div class="Card-bottom-star"><div class="Star is-level-1 is-small is-card"><span class="Star-heart"></span><span class="Star-number">3</span></div></div></div></div></div><div class="SubCards-more"><a href="https://platzi.com/comentario/1059755/" target="_blank"><span>Ver m√°s respuestas</span></a></div></div></div><div class="Card"><div class="Card-top"><div class="Card-top-left"><figure class="Card-top-badge"><img src="./Historia_files/jsparra945_44e302c0-e900-42c4-aa41-7c319e98fce4.webp" alt="jsparra945"></figure><div class="Card-top-name">jsparra945</div><div class="Card-top-role">Estudiante</div></div><div class="Card-top-right"><span class="Card-top-right-dot">¬∑</span><span>el mes pasado</span></div><a class="Card-anchor" href="https://platzi.com/comentario/1057904/" target="_blank"></a></div><div class="Card-middle"><div class="Card-content"><p>‚Äìglobal use word<br>

  function b64DecodeUnicode(str) {
      // Going backwards: from bytestream, to percent-encoding, to original string.
      return decodeURIComponent(atob(str).split('').map(function(c) {
          return '%' + ('00' + c.charCodeAt(0).toString(16)).slice(-2);
      }).join(''));
  }
